           function setRefineByCookie(refineByTypes) {

          function ptk(st,p) {
document.cookie = 'PTK="tk=1f204blid3o6g001&type=jobsearch&subtype=' + st + (p ? '&' + p : '')
 + (st == 'pagination' ? '&fp=1' : '')
+'"; path=/';

         <script type="text/javascript">
          function pclk(event) {
var evt = event || window.event;
var target = evt.target || evt.srcElement;
var el = target.nodeType == 1 ? target : target.parentNode;
var tag = el.tagName.toLowerCase();
if (tag == 'span' || tag == 'a') {
ptk('pagination');
}
return true;
}
function addPPUrlParam(obj) {
var pp = obj.getAttribute('data-pp');
var href = obj.getAttribute('href');
if (pp && href) {
obj.setAttribute('href', href + '&pp=' + pp);
}
}
         </script>
